This will be used as a basic effort to promote the League of Nations' understanding of Manchuria. As for the so-called compromise plan claimed by the League of Nations, the Japanese government seems to avoid actively suggesting the plan, but the Japanese representative Yue will imply in the debate what kind of plan can be promised by Japan. However, the maximum compromise plan that Japan can obtain seems to be that the League of Nations will suspend the conclusion of the report for a certain period of time, at least about a year, and place a so-called period of watching Manchuria. Therefore, it is not difficult to predict the opinions of the Foreign Ministry here.

▲ According to a Japan United News Agency dispatch from Tokyo on the 13th, the League of Nations authorities recently made an important proposal on resolving the Sino-Japanese issue, which was sent to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Therefore, in order to improve the future Sino-Japanese issue, the League of Nations will discuss effective measures based on this principle at the League of Nations General Assembly, and Japan will conduct discussions at the League of Nations General Assembly based on this principle.

International Committee Air

Tokyo, 13th, Dentsu News Agency: Recently, there have been widespread rumors in China that the foreign envoys stationed in China have proposed the establishment of an international committee to assist in resolving the Sino-Japanese negotiations on the Manchurian issue, or that the Lytton Commission would participate in direct Sino-Japanese negotiations. Upon receiving this information, Japanese diplomatic authorities expressed the following views: The actions of the League of Nations are still unclear, yet the Chinese envoy group has formally put forward such a concrete proposal, which is highly suspicious. If this is true, then this proposal must have been based on the achievements of the four-nation envoys' mediation of the Sino-Japanese ceasefire negotiations after the Shanghai Incident. However, the nature of the Shanghai Incident is completely different from the Manchurian Incident. The Shanghai Incident could accept the persuasion of foreign countries, while the Manchurian issue has always maintained the principle of rejecting the participation of third countries. Even if the Lytton Commission participates in the Sino-Japanese negotiations, it will absolutely not be recognized. Because today, when Manchukuo has become independent and Japan has officially recognized it, anything that conflicts with the existing facts of Manchukuo will be consistently opposed. If a wait-and-see attitude is adopted regarding whether the future development of Manchuria is beneficial to peace in the Far East, then even the establishment of a committee will not be opposed. However, if the establishment of this committee is planned and advocated with the intention of suppressing Japan, it will be resolutely rejected.

Second Sheet

Matsuoka's Utter Nonsense

Paris, 13th, Guomin News Agency: Since the Japanese representative to the League of Nations, Yosuke Matsuoka, arrived in Paris, more than a hundred journalists from various countries have visited him. Their purpose was to explore Japan's position when the League of Nations discusses the Lytton Report. As a result of the interviews, Matsuoka gave each reporter a prepared statement, reiterating the reasons for Japan's military actions in Manchuria. Regarding the Lytton Report, he only stated that some parts were agreed upon by Japan, while the rest were difficult to agree with, and that he would explain the errors Japan believed to exist at the League of Nations. Matsuoka was very cautious in answering the reporters' oral inquiries, only making every effort to publicize the chaotic situation in the Far East, and much of what he said was absurd. Here are a few examples to illustrate the propaganda of the Japanese representative in Europe. For example, Matsuoka told a reporter: "We should know the Far East situation more clearly than the people of the West." He also said that the naval and land forces of the major European and American powers have been in China for 32 years, sometimes used to protect their own interests and their expatriates, and sometimes even used to protect their own officials. The interests of the European and American countries in China are relatively small, so they regard the Chinese situation as accidental and not very important. Japan, however, cannot regard accidental events as very important. He also said that the total number of expatriates in China from European and American countries is far less than that of Japanese expatriates. The situation in China has reached a breaking point, and the September 18th Incident only promoted an action, and the deep-rooted chaos created by some old warlords in China over the years is the background of this action. China's enemy is its own people, not foreigners, etc., doing everything possible to slander in order to cover up their brutal aggression. We must urgently seek ways to deal with it. In addition, Matsuoka reiterated Japan's commitment to peace and upholding the Open Door Policy, and promoted the puppet organization.

▲ Berlin, 13th, Guomin News Agency: The Deutsche Allgemeine Zeitung published today an interview with Mr. Matsuoka, the Japanese representative to Geneva, by its reporter. According to Matsuoka's words to the reporter of the Deutsche Allgemeine Zeitung, Matsuoka's visit to Moscow was only of a personal nature and had no political significance. However, he admitted that he had taken this opportunity to exchange irresponsible opinions with the Soviet authorities in order to promote friendship between Japan and Russia and eliminate various misunderstandings. Mr. Matsuoka further stated that the current Japanese people's understanding of the Soviet Union has improved considerably, and the Soviet Union has gradually expressed understanding of Japan's claims. Therefore, Mr. Matsuoka felt that the goods purchased by the Soviet Union from Japan would gradually increase, such as various Japanese manufactured products and machines, which would be sufficient for the Soviet Union to exploit its resources. Mr. Matsuoka also mentioned the recent Japanese-Russian oil agreement and the service of Japanese engineers on the Siberian railways. Matsuoka expressed disbelief in the panic of various countries that the Soviet Union would seize the world's market from various countries, etc. He said that the Soviet Union now has a population of 160 million, and its current urgent task is to supply the needs of its own people, so the era of competition with the outside world is still too early. When discussing the Manchurian issue, Mr. Matsuoka did his best to defend the recent treaty signed between Japan and the Manchurian puppet state, but he neither denied nor admitted that Japan would provide a huge loan to the puppet state. Mr. Matsuoka only stated that the trade situation in the puppet state was excellent, and that the puppet state's army currently has about 100,000 people, all trained by Japanese officers. Mr. Matsuoka finally stated that the League of Nations is not a suitable organization to judge whether a country should be recognized by another country. The Deutsche Allgemeine Zeitung commented on the above-mentioned remarks of Mr. Matsuoka, saying that Mr. Matsuoka's remarks were too polite. In fact, Matsuoka had in-depth discussions with Litvinov, Karakhan, Radek, etc. in Moscow on the Manchurian issue, and Karakhan may soon visit Japan in person to thank Mr. Matsuoka for his visit, and the conclusion of a new Japanese-Russian treaty may begin to be discussed in the near future.

Strange Phenomenon in Geneva

Troops Defect and Sing the Internationale

Geneva, 13th, Reuters News Agency: Geneva is quiet in the middle of the night. The troops have withdrawn to their camps, and the demonstrators have not come out due to the rain. There are now 10,000 soldiers in Geneva, that is, one soldier for every fifteen residents. Yesterday, most of the crowd, except for a few violent ones, behaved in an orderly manner. The demonstrators outside the barracks were mostly teenagers and students, and there were no angry scenes except for scolding and singing the Internationale. The troops do not seem to pay much attention to the situation here.

▲ Geneva, 12th, Reuters News Agency: The situation is slightly calmer after the riots on Wednesday, but a dangerous situation is brewing in this peaceful city. Due to the tense situation, the Swiss government today continued to transfer two more battalions of troops to the city to defend against the chaotic army. When the troops arrived, the residents of Geneva cursed them. The commander then ordered the use of leather belts to draw water and splash the crowd. The crowd clamored and some wanted to seize the belts. When they heard the soldiers loading bayonets, they did not dare to act. The police used batons to disperse the crowd, and the crowd retreated. Today, a team of troops stationed in Geneva showed friendship to the demonstrators, so the team has been kept under guard in the exhibition hall. However, the soldiers broke the lower glass windows and sang the Internationale, chatting and laughing with the crowd outside the window. The trade union announced a general strike for one day in memory of those who died in the riots on Wednesday. However, the day passed peacefully and no riots occurred. The authorities attach great importance to this situation and have adopted various precautions to maintain order. The demonstrators who died on Wednesday were buried at different times and in different cemeteries in order to prevent the gathering of too many people from becoming uncontrollable. The commander has now issued a statement, effectively placing Geneva in a state of siege. Today, there were socialist demonstrations elsewhere in Switzerland, but there were no major disturbances. When a communist party member who died in the chaos on Wednesday was buried, there was a riot, but it was not serious. The body was wrapped in a red flag and placed in a coffin without a lid. When the funeral procession reached the exhibition hall, the soldiers of the 7th team of Geneva mixed with the demonstrators. The authorities then put the team in stone pipes. At the same time, tram transportation was blocked by demonstrators. The tram company now plans to suspend all operations. Isaac, a member of the Geneva City Council, actively participated in the demonstrations on Wednesday and has been arrested.

▲ Geneva, 12th, Havas News Agency: People are marching everywhere in the streets and alleys here, often numbering between 400 and 3,000, and gunshots are heard from time to time. Some residents are very frightened. A communist party member was killed in an accident yesterday and his funeral was held today. A part of the 7th battalion of soldiers smashed windows along the way and expressed sympathy to the demonstrators who were singing the International Revolutionary Song. Then they marched through the city and cut the ropes of the electric poles on the trams. The commander of the Geneva defense army has transferred the Vaud canton troops originally stationed between Lausanne and Geneva to Geneva. These troops arrived in the city at 7:30 PM.

Indian Round Table Conference

Scheduled to be Held in the British House of Commons on Thursday

Gandhi to Fast to Liberate the Untouchables

London, 13th, Reuters News Agency: The nine Indian representatives to the third session of the Indian Round Table Conference arrived here this afternoon. According to the current schedule, the first meeting is scheduled to be held in the House of Lords on Thursday, at which time the Indian representatives will be formally welcomed and all preparations will be made. From November 21st, daily meetings will be held to consider the various issues listed on the agenda.

▲ Bombay, 12th, Havas News Agency: Gandhi has decided to fast to fight for the untouchables issue, and this decision will be implemented as scheduled and will not be postponed. Gandhi declared that the Indian orthodox faction has no right to exclude 40 million people from society. Gandhi also said that Indians have oppressed the untouchables in the name of religion for hundreds of years. World public opinion should uphold justice to seek the liberation of these ethnic groups. As for the Indian orthodox faction, based on the judgment of the Bombay High Court, they do not allow untouchables to go to temples to pray. However, the British judge declared that the purpose of the court's judgment was purely to prevent disturbances from occurring in front of the temples.

▲ Madras, 12th, Havas News Agency: The British government has levied a punitive tax on the places in India where revolutionary storms have occurred, causing the local people to move away to avoid this tax, especially near Calicut. The residents of these places seem to have unanimously requested the government to implement the Poona Pact by order (note that this agreement was the agreement between the Indians and the untouchables that caused Gandhi to stop fasting) and to abolish the treatment suffered by the untouchable class. However, the British government believes that this issue is related to Indian customs and habits, so it is unwilling to intervene and has rejected the residents' request. Gandhi's followers are dissatisfied with the British government, saying that its policy is aimed at destroying the Indian people's faith in Gandhi. As for the orthodox faction in India, they are concentrating their forces to confront Gandhi. If Gandhi fasts, they will also fast in response. Therefore, the current situation is quite ridiculous, as both sides are retaliating with the same means. The trend of suicide is increasing, and the British government may issue an order to prohibit it. Gandhi's followers plan to lead the untouchables to lie on the ground in front of the temples and fast together, while the orthodox faction gathers in front of the prison where Gandhi lives and threatens to fast in response.

▲ Poona, 12th, Guomin News Agency: Today, Gandhi met with a reporter from the Associated Press in prison and said that if the Guruvayur temple is not opened to allow the untouchables to worship, he will fast again on New Year's Day next year. Gandhi is still thin and haggard at this time, and his physical strength has not fully recovered.

Important News

Japan Discovers a Conspiracy Group

The Independent Youth Society Has Great Influence

Takayama Hidesan Has Close Ties

Smuggling Weapons to Disrupt Our Northeast

The crisis of right-wing movements in Japan is probably greater than the crisis of left-wing movements in fact, because right-wing movements use the name of defeating left-wing movements. In fact, it is not only pulling Japan backwards, but also breaking the status quo and even fundamentally overthrowing parliamentary politics. This is a very obvious fact, but because they have active-duty soldiers behind them, and active-duty soldiers have local veterans' associations behind them, no one dares to ask about it in militaristic Japan. Therefore, Inukai Tsuyoshi was assassinated in broad daylight at the official residence as the current prime minister. Now, almost half a year has passed, and the general public only knows that Inukai was assassinated, but does not know the inside story of why the assassin assassinated Mr. Inukai.

Not long ago, the people who presided over the red looting movement were only three people, and the loss of property was also very limited. Although it caused great unease in Japanese society, the scope was still very small. The recent case that occurred was much bigger. The group that presided over this conspiracy was the "Independent Youth Society," which is not very well-known among right-wing groups. They wanted to assassinate the current Prime Minister Saito Makoto, Minister of the Imperial Household Makino Nobuaki, Minister of the Imperial Household Kido Koichi, and Vice Minister of the Imperial Household Sekiya Kazusaburo during this autumn's grand exercises. They carried pistols to the Kansai area, but were discovered by the police before they could carry out their plan. The process is roughly as follows:

The central figure of the Independent Youth Society is Kodama Yoshio, 24 years old, who is the most capable fighter in the right-wing group. In 1928, he strongly opposed the establishment of the Labor-Farmer Party, submitted a Jianbai Shu directly to the Emperor, and was sentenced to six months of imprisonment.

Okada Rihei is also a strong member of the Independent Youth Society. In 1926, he was particularly angry about the establishment of the American Exclusion Act, so he secretly ran into the American Embassy in Tokyo and tore down the American flag hanging on the roof of the embassy, and then ran away without being arrested. Although the Japanese police later found out, they did not investigate further.

The Independent Youth Society was organized by Kodama with dozens of young people. Its political program is roughly as follows:

"1. Respect the Emperor and love the country as the principle of our actions."

"2. We must reform the capitalist politicians who expose their self-interest."

"3. Eliminate the red thoughts and actions that attempt to reform the national system and eliminate all non-Japanese and evil thoughts."

On the surface, it seems that there are no practical actions, and it is just a thought group that is opposed to a left-wing group, and it is an extremely naive and immature small organization. Especially in recent Tokyo and other major cities, such small organizations are like bamboo shoots after a rain, and there are countless numbers. However, because the authorities have given them shelter, they have become even more fierce. At first, they were only intimidating a few financial capitalists, and it did not seem to be a big danger to the current system. However, the assassination of Inukai was not unrelated to the right-wing groups. The Independent Youth Society that has now been broken up is deeply related to that case. At the same time, Takayama Mitsuru's son, Takayama Hidesan, a senior veteran of the Japanese ronin faction, also has close ties. Therefore, Takayama's residence was also inspected, and even the Tenko-kai was checked. In this way, all the right-wing groups in Japan will inevitably be involved.

This kind of conspiracy is by no means a sudden brewing in a short period of time, nor is it an accidental combination of injustice. Taking the trade managed by Oda Toichi, the owner of the Thirteen Goods Sales and Export Co., Ltd. in Kobe, as an example, since 1927, on the surface, he is a gramophone machine merchant. He uses legal procedures to import pistols from Germany, Hungary, and other countries to Japan. In five years, the number of imports has been 260,000 to 270,000, all of which have been disassembled and used as raw materials for gramophone machines. It is not easy for the customs personnel to detect, and of course it is even more difficult for the police to know. In addition, in collusion with foreign ships, before or after the ships entered the port, they were secretly picked up by small motorboats. In the past five years, the total number of secret transfers has been no less than 500,000. In Japan, a country with order and organization, it has to be said that this is an unprecedented and unheard-of strange thing. According to his own news and police speculation, the vast majority were exported to the three northeastern provinces. It is true that in recent years, Japanese warlords have wanted to make trouble in the Northeast, using poor order as an excuse to advance troops and conquer the Northeast. Therefore, from his right-wing private groups to the people who bear the main responsibility, they all participated in, or at least knew about, this secret trade, and regarded this trade as a major work of aggression. They made every effort to contact the green forest heroes between Bai Shan and Hei Shui to disrupt China's politics, and at the same time used this to support Japanese imperialism's political power in the Northeast. What he didn't expect was that the green forests in the three northeastern provinces turned around and refused to be his running dogs, and even went a step further to fight for national struggle. Even if it is not enough to defeat Japan's rule in the three northeastern provinces and cannot immediately restore the lost land, it can shake Japan's attempt to invade the Northeast and make the so-called "Manchurian puppet state" unstable. Then, his secret trafficking of arms (the pistol alone has 500,000) has already caused great chaos in the Northeast last year's September 18th Incident, and it is still continuing to cause trouble. Unexpectedly, this secret import (weapons) trade, after being sold to the three northeastern provinces, brought many back to Japan. He himself estimates that 230 were secretly transported to Tokyo, and at least 60 or 70 were transferred from the right-wing relationship to the hands of left-wing groups. However, this is only a part of the truth that has been discovered. I am afraid that after a considerable period of time, if the investigation continues, there will be more strange things exposed (Tokyo, November 8, 1932)

Liu Xiang Sends More Troops to Attack Luzhou

Liu Commands the Attack Between Yongchuan and Rongchang

Liu Wenhui Is Stationed in Zizhong to Coordinate and All Parties Defend to the Death

Hankou Correspondence: Liu Xiang previously sent Liao Haitao, Mu Yingzhou, He Chunwu and other four brigades, two airplanes, and two warships to launch a large-scale attack on Luzhou. Liu Wenhui's troops rose up to resist in order to maintain the resources, and the battles have been fierce and unprecedented for days. One side attacks and the other defends, with great sacrifices. On the 8th, one warship of the Chongqing army was destroyed by the Chengdu army, and one airplane was shot down. The Chongqing army retreated slightly. Upon hearing the news, Liu Xiang ordered two brigades, including Guo Xun, to join the front line. Together with the previous ones, there were a total of six teams, and the entire second team of airplanes was dispatched to bomb along the city. At the same time, they attacked fiercely with artillery. On the evening of the 10th, more than a dozen places in the city caught fire, and the city walls were almost breached. Fortunately, Liu Wenhui's reinforcements arrived and cooperated to defend to the death. By late at night, both sides still maintained their original front lines. On the 11th, the contact continued, and there was still no victory or defeat. Luzhou has always been known as a dangerous place. The Chengdu army has heavy troops stationed at Guanyizui, Dahejie, and along the river, as well as at Zhongshan Shangguanshi, Xiaoguanmen, and Chenjiaba outside the city, and has built strong fortifications. It is very difficult for the Chongqing army to attack upwards. However, it is rumored that Lantianba and Wufengling have been occupied by the Chongqing army. Whether this is reliable remains to be verified. In addition to sending a large army to attack Luzhou, Liu Xiang also has heavy troops attacking Neijiang and Fushun. In Fushun, the two divisions of Pan Wenhua and Tang Shizun are fighting fiercely with Zhang's brigade and the Qingxiang army in the Huangjiachang, Daijia Temple, and Huaidezhen area, but there has been no progress. In Neijiang, there are Wang Zanxu's division and Li Luo's troops. Wang's division has been holding on to Paimu Town with the Chengdu army for four days. Li Luo has not joined any side. The Chongqing side is vigorously advocating the meeting of Li Luo in Zinei, but this is just to boost morale. Currently, both Liu's attention is focused on Luzhou, Fushun, and Neijiang. Liu Xiang is traveling back and forth between Yongchuan and Rongchang, commanding the various departments to advance. Liu Wenhui is coordinating all parties in Zizhong, strictly ordering them to defend to the death, and never give up Luzhou. Deng Tian, Yang, Li Luo, etc. are currently setting up new defense lines and are taking a wait-and-see attitude towards the war between the two Liu's. It is estimated that once the victory or defeat is determined, they will issue new proposals. (October 12)

Kang-Tibetan Armistice Agreement Signed

Since the outbreak of disputes between Kang and Tibet last year, more than a year has passed. Fortunately, after half a year of bloody battles by the Sichuan-Kang armies, the lost territories of past years were recovered. Since the Tibetan troops retreated, the Sichuan-Kang armies have not pursued them relentlessly. Both sides have held their positions across the Jinsha River and engaged in peace talks. Now, after negotiations between the two sides, a temporary armistice agreement has been reached and signed on October 8th. The content of the agreement is divided into the following six articles: ㈠ The Han and Tibetan sides accept the peace agreement, abandon past grievances, and seek reconciliation. All outstanding Han-Tibetan issues from past years will be resolved by the Central Government and the Dalai Lama. ㈡ The Han army will take the east bank of the upper and lower reaches of the Jinsha River as the foremost defense line. The Tibetan army will take the west bank of the upper and lower reaches of the Jinsha River as the foremost defense line. Neither side's troops shall advance beyond the foremost defense line. ㈢ From October 8th to October 28th of the Chinese calendar (August 9th to August 29th of the Tibetan calendar), the combat troops of both sides shall withdraw separately. The Han army shall retreat east of Ezhide, Ge Baiyu, and Degé. The Tibetan army shall retreat west of Gedengtong, Puwucheng. For the foremost defense line, the Han army shall be stationed in areas such as Dengke, Baiyu, and Degé, while the Tibetan army shall be stationed in areas such as Rendatong and Puwucheng. The number of troops stationed by each side in each location shall not exceed 200, and each side shall send personnel to supervise the withdrawal of troops. ㈣ From the date of the armistice and troop withdrawal, traffic between the two sides shall be restored to its original state, and merchants shall be allowed to travel freely, provided that they obtain permits from the respective governments. In accordance with the spirit of respecting Buddhism and protecting the Dharma, both sides shall uniformly maintain and protect temples in Kang and Tibet, as well as lamas and monks residing, practicing, and traveling in both regions. ㈤ From the date of signing of the conditions, each side shall report to their respective governments for record-keeping and common compliance. ㈥ These conditions shall apply to both the Han and Tibetan sides. Any omissions may be revised by the Central Government and the Dalai Lama in the future. The Commander-in-Chief of the Sichuan-Kang Border Defense has sent Deng Xiang, Commissioner of Jiaoliang, and the Dalai Lama has specially appointed Qiong Rang as the Commissioner for Negotiations. The Sichuan-Kang Border Defense Command has appointed Jiang Yuwen as the Commissioner for Liaison and Negotiations. The Dalai Lama has appointed Qi Bu as the Commissioner for Liaison and Negotiations. Signed at the Degé Gangtuo East Bank Negotiation Site on October 8th, the 21st year of the Republic of China (August 9th of the Tibetan calendar, the Year of the Water Monkey). Representatives of the Kangding people: Jia Qingzhen Baima; Representatives of the Daofu people: Ma Qingweng. The Han translator is called Jideng. An additional agreement stipulates that the newly stationed Tibetan troops in the territory west of Ba'an shall withdraw to their original defenses within nine days. The Chinese-Tibetan translator shall return them to the Han side. October 8th, 21st year of the Republic of China (August 9th of the Tibetan calendar). The Dalai Lama's Commissioner for Negotiations, Rang, makes this guarantee. After the signing of these conditions, it is heard that both sides have implemented them according to the agreement, and the Kang-Tibetan dispute is expected to come to a temporary end.

Changshu

Half of the Rent is Allowed to be Retained for County Use. Due to the Japanese invasion of Shanghai, troops gathered in this county and spent a lot of money on defensive works, plus entertainment and other expenses, totaling more than 160,000 yuan. In addition to using local public funds and various reserves, 60,000 yuan was borrowed from various banks. After the end of the military affairs, the provincial government denied it because the county government had not reported it in advance, resulting in the failure to return the huge amount of money. Public funds can be delayed, but commercial loans cannot be delayed. The provincial government collected two months' worth of house rent, and the local authorities petitioned the provincial government to retain all the rent as military money, but were repeatedly rejected by the provincial government. Later, local gentry and representatives of various groups sent Xu Juntan to petition the provincial government and sent Wang, the director of the Finance Bureau, to the province to present the difficult situation. The Finance Department finally agreed to allow half of the unremitted house rent to be retained for county use, and half still needs to be remitted to the province for urgent needs. Yesterday, it was learned that the Finance Department had forwarded the report to the provincial government, which had also approved it. The county has been notified yesterday.

Gaoyou

Bandits Rob the Arms of the Local Militia. In September, the local militia of Sanlangmiao in the sixth district of the county was robbed of several guns by bandits and killed a training officer. Unexpectedly, the other day (9th) at 6:00 p.m., more than 30 bandits poured into the militia团group. Because the militia members were outnumbered, they did not dare to resist, allowing the bandits to rob all the weapons. The group leader has now reported to the团group headquarters of the ninth district.

▲ Helping Boat Capsizes, Seven Lives Lost. The other day (9th), a helping boat from the Lujia Dam in the eleventh district of the county loaded passengers to the city. Unexpectedly, it encountered a storm in the lake and capsized. Other boats tried their best to rescue and rescued more than ten passengers, but seven people drowned.

Rugao

A Colonization Group Comes to Rugao. Miao Bin, a current Central Committee member, He Yushu, director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Industry, and secretaries and commissioners from the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Industry arrived in Rugao from Tong on the afternoon of the 10th. Representatives of various agencies went to the station to welcome them, and it was decided to hold a welcome meeting at Zhongshan Hall at 9:00 a.m. this morning (11th).

▲ Robbery Cases in Juegang. The family of Gu Zhengshou, a farmer in the Xia Manzao Township of Juegang, was suddenly visited by more than a dozen bandits dressed in short shirts and armed with box cannons at about 1:00 a.m. the other night. They were robbed of about four or five hundred yuan worth of foreign cloth, clothes, and other items. Also, the family of a fisherman surnamed Zhang in the 13th district of Juegang was visited by more than a dozen bandits last night. Fortunately, someone escaped and called for help, and the bandits fled in all directions.

Hangzhou

The Prosecutor Appeals the Xu Zhuoran Case. The case of Xu Zhuoran of Fujian being killed by bandits was transferred to the Hangzhou County Local Court for trial. Chen Yanxiang, Ye Caizhen, and Chen Delin were acquitted, and Lin Luo was sentenced to four years of imprisonment for illegally possessing firearms. Later, the garrison in Fujian Province captured Lin Min, the real culprit who assassinated Xu, in Tongan and sent him to Zhejiang for interrogation, who was also said to have been killed. The Hangzhou Local Court reopened the trial and concluded that there was insufficient evidence, and Lin Min was acquitted of the murder on the 4th of this month. Yesterday, it was learned that Liu Rongjie, the prosecutor in charge of the case, disagreed with the original verdict of Lin Min's innocence and filed an appeal with the Zhejiang High Court, stating his reasons.

Ningbo

Two Robbery Cases ㈠ The family of Liang Xingshan, a resident of Miaojia Bridge in the southeast乡township, claimed to be well-off. Yesterday (12th) was the wedding day for his son, and guests were pouring in. At about 10:00 p.m., relatives and friends were playing a game of方城mahjong when more than a dozen bandits suddenly broke into the house with sharp weapons. It is estimated that they robbed about 500 yuan worth of gold jewelry, clothes, and other items. ㈡ The Tianyuan Temple in Yuyao was suddenly visited by more than a dozen bandits at 11:00 p.m. the other night. After entering the temple, they immediately robbed it, stealing about 600 yuan worth of silver dollars, clothes, and other items.

Xiuning

The Local Militia Rescues a Kidnapped Victim. On the morning of the 4th of this month, Li Hao, a wealthy man in Guangshanling (70 li from Jucheng) near Xiuning, was kidnapped by many bandits towards Kaihua, Zhejiang. His family rushed to the Gulin Local Militia to request assistance. Huang, the Director of the Militia, personally led four militia members to pursue them from Wucheng Youzha to the Jiangtian area on the border of Xiuyi. They saw the bandits carrying the victim and ordered to open fire, exchanging shots. The bandits were unable to resist and abandoned the victim, fleeing in all directions. The victim was escorted home.

Lu Wenxia Wins the 13-Mile Race Walking Championship

丨 Time: 1 Hour, 53 Minutes, 55 Seconds丨

丨 Team First丨 Shanghai West Team Wins 16 Points

丨Women's Champion丨 Cheng Xianzhi First in One Mile

The Shanghai Chinese Open 13-Mile Race Walk took place yesterday morning in a very enthusiastic atmosphere. Lu Wenxia started from the intersection of Carter Road and Jing'an Temple Road and was the first to reach the finish line inside the Chinese Athletic Field with a time of 1 hour, 53 minutes, and 55 seconds. The Shanghai West Team A won 16 points, and Lu was a member of the Shanghai West Team, so Shanghai West won a double championship. Cheng Xianzhi set a new record of 11 minutes and 52/5 seconds in the unprecedented women's one-mile race walk. After the competition, the prizes were distributed, which were rich and beautiful. It did not end until noon.

Circumstances Along the Way

At the starting point, a grand and impressive sight. At 7:50 AM, a line was formed at the intersection of Carter Road. After roll call, Zhang Xinfu fired a shot from his signal gun, and hundreds of swift feet took off together, heading straight for Jing'an Temple. The long, snaking line then divided into front and rear sections. Passing Jing'an Temple, which was one mile away, Zhang Zaojiu led the pack, followed by Ge Jinwen, Zhang Zhihe, Chen Liwen, Lü Chongyi, Yao Yaxin, Lü Wenxia, and others. It was still too early to tell who would ultimately come out on top.

▲ Xu Aichen Initially Takes the Lead, then Zhang Zhihe Surpasses Zhang Zaojiu to Take First Place. Lü Wenxia, Xu Aichen, Ge Jinwen, and Zhang Zaojiu were neck and neck, almost reaching Zhaofeng Garden. Xu Aichen then overtook Zhang Zhihe, taking the lead by a distance of thirty yards, exhibiting a superior form and great potential for victory. Thus, he had smooth sailing until a change occurred on the Avenue Petain.

▲ A Glimpse of the Hongqiao Road: Guangfeng Garden was at the two-and-a-half-mile mark. Turning from Route Pelliot and entering Hongqiao Road marked six miles, half of the entire race. No significant changes occurred within these three miles. Ge Jinwen and Lü Wenxia lagged slightly behind, placing Zaojiu in third. At the Lincoln Road intersection, Zaojiu overtook Zhang Zhihe again, securing second place. Xu Aichen, however, consistently maintained the lead. Guiding the way into Hongqiao Road, Zhang Zhihe fell back to fifth. At that time, the order of the leaders was: (1) Xu Aichen, (2) Zhang Zaojiu, (3) Lü Wenxia, (4) Ge Jinwen, (5) Zhang Zhihe. It seemed that the individual and team championships were largely decided, as Zhang, Lü, and Ge were all top athletes from the Shanghai West District.

▲ Changes on Avenue Petain: As the racers advanced, passing the Tong De Girls' School and Jiaotong University, and then turning north onto Avenue Haig and heading southwest again on Avenue Petain, the championship situation underwent sudden changes. These last three miles saw two major shifts. Ge Jinwen picked up the pace, step by step, overtaking Lü Wenxia and Zhang Zaojiu, and then surpassing Xu Aichen to take the lead. His back-and-forth competition with Xu, with repeated overtaking and falling behind, was arguably the most exciting moment of the entire race. Ge did not relax, staying close behind Xu. As they approached Avenue Albert, Ge once again overtook Xu, taking the lead. Then, Wang Zhaoxiang overtook Zhang Zaojiu, and Zhang Zhihe moved forward.

▲ Competition Approaching the Finish Line: On Route Pichon, heading straight east, the China Athletic Field was already in sight. Ge Jinwen, having overtaken Xu Aichen, now held first place. Lü Wenxia, with increasing momentum, surpassed one after another, challenging Ge Jinwen shoulder-to-shoulder. As expected, Lü flew past Ge, reaching the finish line thirty yards ahead. Xu Aichen finished third, one hundred yards behind Ge. Wang Zhaoxiang, Zhang Zaojiu, Zhang Zhihe, and others followed in close succession.

The Thirteen-Mile Race Team Champion: Shanghai West Team

(Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

A Groundbreaking Achievement for Women

Yesterday marked the realization of the first-ever women's race walking event. Following the men's thirteen-mile race, the women's one-mile race began at eleven o'clock. After roll call, they lined up, and the starting gun was fired. They circled the field four times. However, due to a lack of training, some participants had poor form, and some were running and jumping, leading to Liu Wenjing, despite finishing first, being disqualified for three violations.

▲ No Change in the First Half: From the start, Liu Wenjing sped ahead, demonstrating great speed, raising suspicions of her being paced. This caused her to slow down slightly. Nevertheless, Liu remained in the lead, with Cheng Xianshi close behind. The order of the first three laps saw no changes. The order was: Liu Wenjing, Cheng Xianshi, Zhang Peilun, Huang Zhenqi, Zhang Baojin, Wu Shiying, Ye Ming, Guo Lianni, and others, with distances of two to three feet separating them.

▲ A Pity for Being Disqualified: Upon reaching the finish line, Liu Wenjing and Cheng Xianshi were neck and neck, with Liu Wenjing finishing a mere two inches ahead, followed by Cheng Xianshi. Zhang Baojin surged to third place. However, the referee's decision was that Liu had received three warnings for violations and could not be excused for the first offense, thus had to strictly enforce the rules, disqualifying her and elevating Cheng Xianshi to first place. It was a pity for Liu. Hopefully, she will make another effort next time. The groundbreaking nature of the women's event drew considerable attention from the spectators. The awards were presented by Shen Siliang, and the event concluded.

"Race Walking Training Method" to be Published Soon

Written by Lu Xiangqian 丨 Foreword by Shi Youhui

丨Pictured Demonstrations by Shi Jinsheng, Zhang Zaochi, and Zhou Yuyu

Race walking competition has become popular in China. The Diligent Bookstore at 392 Route Labor神父, Shanghai, has recently commissioned Mr. Lu Xiangqian, chairman of the Shanghai Secondary School Sports Federation, to write "Race Walking Training Method," which details the history, definition, attire, and methods of race walking, as well as basic training, training schedules, competition strategies, race walking rules, and world records for men's and women's race walking. It also includes a brief history of the China Race Walking Team, biographical sketches of race walking athletes, and the regulations of the Shanghai International Race Walking Association. In addition to text, it contains over forty valuable photographs of race walking athletes such as Shi Jinsheng, Zhou Yuyu, and Zhang Zaochi demonstrating correct form. Mr. Shi Youhui, coach of the China Race Walking Team, has written a foreword for the book, highly praising it. The book is priced at six jiao (with a 10% discount). Mail order registration is one jiao and one fen. It is expected to be published on the 20th of this month.

Second Interport Football Trial Match

Mixed Team Comes Out on Top

Scored Both Penalties

Wins 3-2 Against the White Team

Yesterday, the Shanghai Western Football Association held its second interport trial match at the Recreation Ground. Twenty-two top Chinese and Western players from Shanghai were divided into a White team and a Mixed team for a competitive match. Several selection committee members attended to observe and critique, aiming to evaluate talent for potential inclusion in the team and to prevent overlooking promising players. The crowd was smaller than the previous match, and the game was less intense. Unexpectedly, the White team, expected to represent Shanghai, conceded two penalties and ultimately lost 2-3 to the Mixed team, contrary to the selection committee's expectations. Commentators suggested that the referee's excessively critical handling of the two penalties contributed to the White team's defeat. However, the day's performance showed that the Mixed team's forwards were more impressive, especially the right wingers, Kezhi and Chen Jiaqiu, who demonstrated excellent coordination. The White team's defense, on the other hand, appeared stronger.

丨Contributions from Formal Candidates丨

After two trial matches, the general public likely has a good understanding of the formal candidates. However, Chinese and Western viewpoints differ, with the former prioritizing agility and the latter emphasizing strength. Based on observations, here is a suggestion for a potential team for the selection committee to consider:

Chen Zhenhe

Li Ning, He Lei, Mai Sai'er

Zhou Xianyan, Zha Xu, Lao Deng

Stoke, Weisihe, Chen Jiaqiu

Feng Yunyou Ke Zhi

Zhou Xianyan is undoubtedly a capable goalkeeper. David Guren lacks experience and should be a backup. There is a shortage of interior midfielders in Shanghai, and Li Ning, Feng Yunyou, Stoke, and Mai Sai'er are among the best. Li and Feng performed excellently in the first trial match, while Li and Stoke stood out yesterday. Li is certain to secure a central position. The challenge lies in choosing one of Stoke and Feng, so they are listed together for future consideration. Zha Xu is experienced and strong, like Mount Tai. He Lei and Weisihe are versatile and can play on either side. Xu Yahui is fierce and agile, and Zha Xu feels a sense of rivalry with him. Lao Deng is a natural center forward. The interior wing positions deserve consideration. Mai Sai'er, who played as an interior defender yesterday, was formerly a forward and is agile and skillful. He would be better suited for the left interior position than Jack. Chen Jiaqiu controls the ball with ease, providing excellent support on either side. His coordination with Kezhi yesterday was outstanding. He is recommended for the left wing. Chen Zhenhe is unmatched as the right winger. Fa Fange is slow and his shots are inaccurate, unlike Kezhi, who excels at both running and shooting. Based on these observations, here is a proposed lineup.

丨Review of Yesterday's Intense Battle丨

The first half began with the White team playing with ten players, facing pressure from the opposing team. A cross from Kezhi landed in front of the goal, but Gaoshanfu misjudged and shot into the sky. Chen Jiaqiu passed again, but Zhou Xianyan blocked it. Fifteen minutes into the game, White team's Ya'erjie entered the field, boosting morale. Ya'erjie shot from within the crowd, scoring the first goal. The Mixed team maintained momentum and invaded again. De Fei committed a foul, resulting in a penalty. Chen Jiaqiu, entrusted with the team's hopes, shot like an arrow. Zhou touched the ball with both hands, deflecting it onto the goalpost and down. The referee declared it a goal. The first half ended with a score of 1-1.

▲In the second half, Kezhi from the Mixed team was injured and replaced by Baowuerdeng. At that time, the White team showed improvement. Chen Zhenhe and Lao Deng made several attacks, but David defended well. Suddenly, the situation changed. The three players on the left side of the Mixed team simultaneously approached the goal. Goalkeeper Gensheng missed an opportunity to shoot, and the enemy's reinforcements arrived, negating the effort. The Mixed team attacked again, and Gaoshanfu failed to block the shot, resulting in another goal. After losing the lead, the White team regained momentum. He Lei was blocked and passed the ball to Chen Zhenhe, who then passed it to Fa Fange. Fa Fange dribbled the ball and created an opportunity for Lao Deng to score, tying the game 2-2. Soon after, Tang Boni, carrying the ball, was tripped, resulting in another penalty for the White team. Chen Jiaqiu, with familiarity, scored again. As the sun set, the game ended, with the Mixed team winning 3-2.

Important News

The Chinese Children's Education Society's Annual Meeting Concludes

丨Election of Directors丨 Next Annual Meeting Scheduled for Beijing or Jinan

The third annual meeting of the Chinese Children's Education Society lasted for three days, with the 13th being the last day. According to the annual meeting agenda, the second day was for discussing proposals, and today was for discussing society affairs. A total of 36 proposals were on the agenda, excluding impromptu motions. Yesterday, only five proposals related to health education in the first category and one proposal related to curriculum, teaching materials, and textbook research in the second category were discussed. Including impromptu motions, there were still over 30 proposals remaining (including proposals for discussing society affairs). Today, according to the agenda, there was a visit to the Central Meteorological Observatory and the History Museum at 1:00 PM, and a reception hosted by the Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau at Wuzhou Park and a banquet hosted by the Central Party Headquarters at 3:00 PM. Therefore, the meeting in the morning needed to proceed at a particularly fast pace. Fortunately, a Health Education Committee had been formed yesterday regarding health education, and a Textbook Research Committee had been formed regarding curriculum, teaching materials, and textbook research. All proposals of the same nature or those that did not require excessive research could be grouped together and submitted to the committees for review and research, thereby providing a solution.

Details of Proposal Discussions

The meeting began at approximately 9:00 AM, with Tian Shuren as the master of ceremonies and Li Qingsong as the chairman. It was reported that the discussion of society affairs would be advanced. Proposals for society affairs could be divided into four categories: (1) the location of the next annual meeting, (2) the central issue for the next annual meeting, (3) issues related to improving the daily affairs of the society, and (4) issues related to adding new ventures. Regarding the first category, there were two proposals: (1) the next annual meeting should be held in Beijing and Jinan, and (2) the location of the society's annual meeting should be selected in an area farther from the society's central location in order to promote interest in children's education. (These were discussed together.) The chairman also reported that a telegram had been received from Fuzhou, stating that the climate was suitable and the scenery was beautiful, which was submitted for reference. As a result of the discussion, the first location for the next meeting was Beijing, and the second location was Jinan (if Beijing was not possible, it would be changed to Jinan). Regarding the second category, the central issues were: (1) the society should focus on civic training in the next year, and the fourth annual meeting should discuss and exhibit civic training cases. Heike Tan explained the reasons for the proposal. Zheng Xiaocang said that while civic training was the focus, special attention should be paid to history, and there were many areas of history that needed to be improved. Ma Jingxuan said that attention should be paid to national salvation education, expressing the national spirit and enabling society to understand thoroughly, and advocated for modifying the wording of the proposal. Xue Tianhan asked whether the research center issue was consistent with the exhibition center. The chairman reported that it was consistent. Luo Tingguang believed that civic training covered a wide range of content and did not need to be revised. Jiang Xicen and Shi Shifu argued that the research center of the previous session should not necessarily be the exhibition center of the next session, because after research, results would be obtained before determining the exhibition center, which would be better. Jiang advocated using textbooks as the center, and Shi advocated using the national language as the center. Ma Kehan said that in order to make the outside world understand the meaning of children's education, he still advocated using civic training as the center. Huang Jianzhong agreed with using civic training as the center and added that attention should be paid to six aspects of civic knowledge: (1) enabling children to understand national culture, (2) civic morality, (3) social organization, (4) national politics, (5) national law, and (6) national economy. He also said that the distribution and coordination of civic education materials in schools at all levels should be noted, and materials suitable for our national culture should be determined by referring to foreign situations. Ren Jian and Chen Jianqi proposed using production education as the center and said that production education was the most important goal of civic education. Wu Yanren said that the current first problem was the word "center," and no more details should be discussed other than the center. Xue Tianhan reported that the knowledge portion of civic training determined this time had been extracted and included in a separate subject area, which was smaller. Luo Tingguang said that only those related to children's education should be discussed, and the rest could be ignored. The chairman summarized the opinions, and the so-called central issues were (1) civic training, (2) textbooks (bird and animal languages attached), and (3) production education. Wu Yanren said that there was no need to call it a central issue, call it the points to pay attention to in the first, second, and third categories. Xia Zhanchu summarized and suggested that from this year to the opening of next year's meeting, research should be conducted on issues such as civic training, textbooks, and production education, and the next exhibition should focus on civic training. Wu Yanren said that the meaning of civic training was too narrow and should be changed to civic education. Chen Heqin advocated exhibiting all three. Dong Mengjian advocated still using the center because it was a research center, not a discussion center. (Discussion Result)

Maintaining the central issue as civic training (38 voted for production education, 31 for textbooks, and 21 for civic training). Following Xia Zhanchu's suggestion, three approaches were taken, and following Chen Heqin's opinion, attention was paid to all three exhibitions simultaneously. Election of Directors

Ma Ketan temporarily proposed that the supervisory committee should be organized due to the organization of the Executive Committee. It is proposed to change the executive committee to the board of directors. The chairman reported that the results of the election of directors were that the Nanzhong Primary School (108 votes), the Central District Experimental School (84 votes), the China University Experimental School (78 votes), and the China University College of Education (74 votes) (were elected). The Girls' Middle School Primary School (70 votes), Suzhou Middle School Experimental Primary School (62 votes), and Shanghai No. 1 Experimental Primary School (41 votes) (were nominated). Individual directors were Chen Heqin (133 votes), Ma Ketan (81 votes), Zheng Xiaocang (74 votes), Xia Chengfeng (66 votes), and Dong Renjian (65 votes) (were elected). Wu Yanren (58 votes), Li Qingsong (41 votes), Shen Yushan (31 votes), Shi Renfu (19 votes), and Luo Tingguang (18 votes) (were nominated). According to regulations, both groups and individuals who were elected should resign one seat, so Ma Ketan of Nanzhong Primary School resigned his individual seat, and Wu Yanren succeeded him.

Last Night's Central Banquet

丨 The Municipal Social Bureau Holds a Tea Party

Nanjing, 13th: At 3 PM on the 13th, the Municipal Social Bureau of Nanjing hosted a tea party for members of the Children's Education Association at Wuzhou Park, presided over by Wang Chongzhi. In the evening, the Central Government hosted a banquet for the members at the Huarui Reception Hall, with Ju Zheng delivering a welcome speech. During the banquet, Chen Guofu spoke at length about the necessary directions for improving primary school education: 1. Health education should be linked to children's families, and it is easier to achieve results by educating their mothers. 2. Primary school subjects are too numerous, and children's physical and mental states are too fragile to bear the burden. Schools should only teach essential knowledge that can be applied flexibly, such as focusing on nationalism in teaching materials when the country is in distress. Other subjects, such as stories and party knowledge, can be taught by families. 3. The content of existing children's literature is poor, cultivating a deep impression in children of seeking personal gain and forgetting that they are individuals of the nation. He hopes to correct this and make full use of examples of inherent culture in Chinese history to compile fairy tales, cultivating children to become children of the Chinese nation. Shao Yuan Chong spoke about how primary school education should adapt to children's individual personalities and guide them accordingly, focusing on the basic education of national character and correcting individual shortcomings. Finally, Zheng Xiaocang, a representative of the members, delivered a reply. The event concluded happily around 8 PM.

Local News

Municipal Bureau of Education

Banning Unqualified Party Doctrine Teachers

A Circular Order to All Schools for Strict Compliance

The Municipal Bureau of Education issued an instruction yesterday to all levels of schools in the city, stating: "Regarding the letter No. 135 from the Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipal Committee of the Kuomintang of China, the Third District Party Department reported that, after reviewing the files taken over, the Eighth District Representative Congress submitted a case to rectify the employment of Party Doctrine teachers in the city. After investigation, there are numerous registered and qualified Party Doctrine teachers in the city, but many schools at all levels still employ unregistered and unqualified teachers, and have not given preferential treatment to those who have been registered and qualified. This matter has been submitted to the Executive Committee meeting for the second time for resolution, and a formal request is hereby submitted to your committee to instruct the Bureau of Education to order school principals to give priority to employing registered and qualified Party Doctrine teachers for the convenience of the Party. Therefore, in order to promote Party Doctrine education, unqualified teachers must be strictly banned. A special letter is hereby issued for your review and handling." In response to the above, after investigation, all schools must employ certified qualified personnel as Party Doctrine teachers, as previously ordered by the Bureau. This letter is issued in addition to the reply and outward distribution, ordering the relevant schools to strictly comply with the above.

Second Day of the Jiangsu Secondary School Science Conference

The Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Science Conference was held at the Shanghai Provincial Shanghai High School. The morning was spent discussing motions, and the afternoon was spent on inspections, as reported in this newspaper yesterday. The conference continued today, still presided over by Shen Yizhen of Shanghai High School, with Xu Renwu as the recorder. The resolutions are as follows: (6) The motion to stipulate the practical teaching program for high school science courses and the motion for science equipment are to be discussed together. (7) Request the Ministry of Education to promptly promulgate the translated names of science terms to unify and facilitate teaching. (8) Suggest that the Jiangsu Secondary School Federation hold a periodic science achievement exhibition. (9) Organize a committee to study the science curriculum outline and compile standard tests, and request the Provincial Education Federation to ask several schools to take on the responsibility separately. (10) Formulate the minimum standards for science equipment in secondary schools. For junior and senior high schools, the draft formulated by Shanghai High School will be distributed to various schools for comments. For rural normal schools, Wu Jiang Rural Normal School is recommended to formulate a unified submission to the Provincial Education Federation for further discussion by several school officials responsible for review and revision. (11) Request the Education Department to designate temporary funds to subsidize students from various schools to visit industrial factories and transportation agencies regularly to facilitate science education. (12) Increase opportunities for teachers' research, such as visits, exchanges of writings, and holding scientific education discussion meetings during holidays. Various schools should try their best to implement these measures. (13) The date and location of the next meeting will be decided by the Provincial Education Federation. In addition to the motions discussed and inspections, Shanghai High School Principal Zheng Xigu, the Science Society of China, and the Practical Science and Arts Museum hosted banquets for all the representatives, and everyone enjoyed themselves.

Great China Middle School Forms a Volunteer Army Donation Team

In view of the urgent need for relief for the brave and loyal volunteer army in Northeast China resisting Japan, the affiliated middle school of Great China University in Western Shanghai has entrusted students Chen Jiaren, Xia Xiru, Ji Juan, and others (nine in total) as donation committee members through a school affairs meeting. The donation team is actively soliciting donations from all sectors, and the results are already considerable. It is reported that the school authorities have also established donation incentive regulations to encourage them.

Commercial News

Finance

Slight Fluctuations in the Gold Market Last Week

丨 British and American Exchange Rates Initially Increased, Then Decreased 丨

The standard gold price fluctuated slightly last week, starting weak and then sharp, but then seemed to decline, but without excessive turbulence. The daily difference was at most six or seven taels. It happened to be the Western merchant autumn races, and the market only traded for two full days, and the psychology of the industry was hesitant and uncertain, so the supply and demand were divergent. Initially, the silver market reported an increase, and Shanghai's exchange bills were loose and abundant, so it was expected to decline. The opening price of 744 taels and 7 qian only decreased by 2 qian. Then, due to the dumping by the Guangdong merchants, it broke down by 40 taels. The next day, a low price of 734 taels and 3 qian suddenly appeared. Afterwards, it slightly fluctuated because the news of the US election was that Roosevelt was elected. According to Roosevelt's advocacy of raising silver prices, people's hearts turned downward to prevent the rise in silver prices. The gold price once went downstream, but the exchange market was calm, both overt and covert. Moreover, the Central Bank released spot goods, so the price was able to hold steady. On Thursday, unexpectedly, the silver price was reported to have fallen, while the exchange bills were still tight. The industry sought to close out short positions, and general short sellers rushed to cover, causing the price to soar, and Meng Jin suddenly exceeded the 750 taels mark. The autumn races were over, and full-day trading resumed. However, by the evening market, due to the tendency of Guangdong merchants to sell, the price fell. As a result, it soared by 12 taels and 9 qian compared to the previous day. The day before, it rose and fell, and the changes in the market were unexpected. The silver market was near falling and far flat, and people's hearts seemed to soften. Finally, 46 taels and 3 qian were seen. In an instant, the buyers were slightly more diligent, and the market was able to stabilize. The US dollar tended to be popular, and a sharp surge to a peak of 753 taels and 7 qian forced the silver market to deviate, and the British market shrank, and the American market was flat. However, private telegraphs and forward prices rose instead, especially the exchange rate soared, and the gold market fell due to the environment. It should have returned to the 50 taels level, but it was 44 taels and 1 qian in the end. The final easing trend resulted in 46 taels and 7 qian. However, after the close, due to the entry of scattered short positions, it rebounded to 48 taels and some change. The total comparison shows that the price rebounded by 1 tael and 8 qian compared to the previous Saturday. The high and low prices of the entire week differed by 19 taels and 4 qian (the difference between the opening and closing prices was 2 taels). As for spot goods, the Central Bank released and opened a total of about 1,000 bars of bare gold. Initially, 11 taels and a half were added, but later only 10 taels and 0.025 were counted. All the swap positions for November were initially more than 2 taels, but later only 7 qian and 5 fen were counted, and they have been mostly closed out. As for the overseas silver market, it has risen for three consecutive weeks and then slightly declined. The local exchange market has only shrunk by half a level for British gold (125), and the American gold is flat. The internal market initially increased and then decreased, and then tended to be flat, but it was also slightly different due to the exchange rate fluctuations. Among the Chinese gold businesses, the supply exceeded the demand. Currently, the US dollar is short about 2.3 million yuan. There are gold price hedges, and the pound sterling is short more than 200,000 pounds. As for the settlement price, it was initially pressed down to more than 70 taels, then later around 70 taels, and then around 60 taels. It is likely that the exchange rate continued to rise. This week, the overall increase and decrease was calculated as a 3-cent increase for British against US and a 1.9375-cent increase for American against British. Now, the high and low prices of the silver market and exchange bills are listed below:

Category Highest Lowest Compared to Last Saturday

Large Bars, Forward Term Eighteen pence, five Eighteen pence, one three five Shrinking by zero six two five

The Discount Market Is Becoming More Stable

Yesterday was a Sunday, a bank holiday, so the general atmosphere and trading conditions were generally flat and unremarkable. The silver discount rate did not fluctuate much. The early market was 7 qian, 0 li, 9 hao, 8 hu, and 7 si. The afternoon market was 7 qian, 0 li, 9 hao, 6 hu, and 2 si. As a result, the difference between the two markets was only 2 hao and a half. The silver discount rate was 3 fen in both markets, and it was similar to the previous day. The volume of exchange and bill transactions was 70,000 yuan in the early market and 20,000 yuan in banknotes. The volume of exchange and bill transactions was 170,000 yuan in the afternoon market and 50,000 yuan in banknotes. There were no transactions outside the market. The total volume of discount bill transactions in both markets was about 5 million yuan. Private banks received and delivered more than 24 million, and public banks received and delivered more than 6.7 million. Small private banks traded more than 200,000 yuan. The Jiangnan small silver dollar was 6 qian, 1 fen, and 6 li in both the early and afternoon markets. Only 3,000 jiao were traded in the early market. The Guangdong small silver dollar was 6 qian, 0 li, 2 hao, 7 si and a half in the early market, and 6 qian, 0 li, 3 hao, 2 si and a half in the afternoon market. 65,000 jiao were traded in the early market and 35,000 jiao were traded in the afternoon market. Copper coins increased by 4,000 wen to 409,000 wen.

Securities

The Prosperity of the Bond Market Last Week

丨Total Weekly Turnover Exceeded 50 Million Yuan丨

丨Prices Rose Significantly, with Large and Frequent Fluctuations丨

Over the past week (from November 7th to 12th), the spot market conditions of various bond maturities at the Chinese Securities Exchange showed little activity in spot trading. A total of 112,000 yuan was opened, including 33,000 yuan of 19 Customs, 14,000 yuan each of Financial 20 Customs, 12,000 yuan of Reorganization Heritage, and only a few thousand yuan of others. However, the futures market was quite lively, and the market sentiment remained very active. Major players were no longer as sluggish as before, and both near and far-term transactions were brisk. The market's prosperity was the best seen this year, mainly because bond prices fluctuated greatly last week, and the overall environment also experienced some changes. The daily turnover was highest on Thursday, reaching over 15.4 million yuan, followed by 9.74 million yuan on Wednesday and over 8 million yuan on Tuesday. The other days each recorded 5.6 to 6.2 million yuan. The total turnover for the week was 50.04 million yuan, including 33.12 million yuan for November maturities and 16.92 million yuan for December maturities, exceeding the previous week by 24.9 million yuan. Among them, Unified Salt Tax was the most active, with 7.67 million yuan for November maturities and 4 million yuan for December maturities. Unified Tax had 5.475 million yuan for November maturities and 3.13 million yuan for December maturities. Other notable figures include 4.215 million yuan for November maturities and 2.43 million yuan for December maturities of 20 Customs, 3.275 million yuan for November maturities and 2.02 million yuan for December maturities of 20 Rolled, 3.02 million yuan for November maturities and 2.4 million yuan for December maturities of Demobilization, 3.485 million yuan for November maturities and 1.315 million yuan for December maturities of 19 Customs, 2.68 million yuan for November maturities and 1.09 million yuan for December maturities of 19 Charity, 1.535 million yuan for November maturities and 490,000 yuan for December maturities of Customs Reorganization Heritage, 755,000 yuan for Customs, and 809,600 yuan for Reorganization 6 Li, with only 245,000 yuan traded for November maturities and 10,000 yuan for Financial. In general, the trend of bond prices in the past week, although the situation did not see major progress in the first half of the week, and diplomatic relations with Japan remained in an unresolvable state, the market, considering the peaceful resolution of the Shandong issue and the generally favorable situation, led to a good market sentiment, with investment buyers becoming increasingly active. The attitude of financial institutions also gradually improved, and major players were not as indifferent as before, resulting in a consistent surge in prices. Monday saw an increase of 60 to 70 cents to 1.30 to 1.40 yuan, Tuesday saw another increase of several cents to 1 yuan, and Wednesday saw an even stronger surge, with Reorganization 6 and Financial rising sharply by 3 yuan, Demobilization continuing to rise by 2 yuan, and others rising by 1 yuan to 1.60 to 1.70 yuan. However, the sharp rise in market prices was driven by temporary market sentiment rather than a genuine major development in the overall environment, leading to a strong reaction. On Thursday, the excessive price increases prompted those with goods to sell, and a certain party released a large amount, resulting in an oversupply and a sharp drop in prices of 1 to 2.30 to 2.40 yuan. On Friday, only Unified Salt Tax rose by about 1 yuan, with minor fluctuations in other areas. The weekend saw a consistent decline, but only by about 40 to 50 cents. By this point, the market situation was nearing its end. Although market trading remained active, it seemed to be dominated by swap transactions. Observing the trend, unless there are other major changes, there are unlikely to be major fluctuations in the near future. Yarn and Cotton

The Yarn Market Was Lifeless Last Week

Cotton yarn has remained stagnant and weak for the past week due to sluggish actual demand and tight monetary conditions. The various trading groups have shown little vitality. In addition, yarn dumping in the Yangtze River region and the ongoing war in Sichuan have further impacted local yarn, leading to weak market sentiment and increased short selling. However, Rongxing, a major player, has been trying its best to resist. Nevertheless, the current situation is such that actual sales are too slow, and upward momentum is minimal. Fortunately, the bottom has dried up, and the mills have not accumulated excessive inventory. The market situation is lifeless, but sellers remain optimistic, believing that prices cannot fall. Therefore, new short sellers have eagerly entered the market. According to statistics, the total purchases by various trading groups throughout the week were only 2,962 bales. The market was sluggish, and the price of standard yarn fell by 2.3.4.6 cents compared to the previous week. The total turnover for the week was 136,600 bales. Signs of a Turnaround in the Cotton Market

There are signs of a turnaround and upward movement in the cotton market. Although the situation for American cotton is unfavorable, the market has been fluctuating within a certain range this week. Therefore, some market participants are inclined to buy. In addition, prices in various production areas are also difficult to lower. As a result, those with actual goods are hedging, making it more difficult for the market to decline. As for the large amount of cotton that a certain manufacturer released, it is currently observing the prices in various regions and is unwilling to release more. Instead, it is considering covering its positions when prices fall. Therefore, if American cotton can stabilize, there are concerns that local cotton will not decline further. However, due to sluggish yarn sales and weak demand from mills, the future remains uncertain. Arrivals at the wharves include 3,539 bales of Yao cotton and 8,206 bales of Tong cotton. Silk and Tea Autumn Race Concurrence and Mid-Term Silk Market Report

丨Early in the Week, Telegraphs Turned Silent, Silk Merchants Took Advantage of Low Prices to Purchase Raw Silk丨

丨At the Weekend, Japanese Silk Prices Soared, and the European and American Silk Markets Gradually Became Active丨

Last week, the local foreign silk market coincided with the mid-term of the Autumn Racing Season. In the first half of the week, all foreign firms were closed in the afternoon, and the market was only open for three and a half days throughout the week. In addition, although the political and economic unrest in New York and Lyon had subsided, the abundant silk inventory did not stimulate demand, and the telegrams turned silent. The price of Shanghai White Filature had fallen back to the lowest level seen in June and July of this year. Therefore, silk factories in Hangzhou, Shaoxing, Huzhou, and Jiaxing took advantage of the low prices to purchase raw silk for winter silk fabrics. Although silk sales were not quiet, silk prices remained low. However, in the second half of the week, Japanese silk prices in Yokohama and Kobe soared by 43 Japanese yen per picul. The news spread to the European and American markets, and the silk market gradually became active. New York Japanese silk prices soared by several tens of cents per pound, and Shanghai White Filature also rose by 8 to 9 cents. Lyon Japanese silk prices rose by 6 to 7 francs, and Chinese silk factory dry spun silk prices rose by 4 to 5 francs (per kilogram). Unfortunately, silk sales were sluggish, and Japanese silk prices at the weekend showed signs of weakening again. This was because Yokohama Japanese silk futures prices fell back by more than ten Japanese yen last Friday. After a sharp decline, it may be difficult to stabilize. Last week, Shanghai silk merchants traded more than 200 bales of raw silk, and exported more than 400 bales of raw silk.
